The Higher Branch Announces the Registration Methods for Lawyers 171

Xu Weizhen, the president of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, issued the second announcement yesterday, stating the matter of the announcement. The Ministry of Judicial Administration issued Order No. 660, stating that in the case of lawyers applying for registration, they must attach two recent two-and-a-half-inch half-length photos. The Ministry has previously stipulated the methods and issued them to all provinces on March 10th of this year for compliance. It is found that these methods apply equally to foreign lawyers who are executing the duties of lawyers in the court and the Shanghai Special District Local Court under its jurisdiction when applying for registration. The Order No. 572 of the Order of Examination is re-examined and sent to the hospital for compliance and transfer for compliance, this order. It is also declared that the Committee of Examination of Lawyers has issued Order No. 572, stating that the chairman of the Committee of Examination of Lawyers, Xie Yingzhou, has submitted a report for advice. At the 73rd meeting on March 4 of this year, the committee discussed the case of applicants for examination who must attach photos in the future for identification and easy reference. It was decided that all applicants for examination or those who apply for a lawyer's license must attach two recent two-and-a-half-inch photos in addition to submitting proof of qualification documents and fees in accordance with the regulations. One copy will be kept by the department for future reference, and one copy will be attached to the lawyer's license. When registering with the higher court of each province, two or three photos should also be submitted (two for those who execute duties in a local court, and three for those who execute duties in two local courts). One photo will be attached to the lawyer's register, and the rest will be sent by the higher court to the local court designated to execute the duties of a lawyer for future reference. If the registrant is holding a lawyer's license previously obtained, four or five photos should be added (four for those who execute duties in a local court, and five for those who execute duties in two local courts) and submitted to the higher court for attachment, storage, and presentation. A courtyard seal should be added to all places where photos are attached to the lawyer's license. All those who have a lawyer's license and have already registered must add photos in accordance with the above regulations within three months from the date of announcement of the higher court of each province, and present them to the higher court of each province for separate processing. Those who have not registered should also add two photos within the time limit and submit them to the Ministry or present them to the higher court for verification, etc. In this regard, it is found that the proposed methods are still feasible, except

In addition to notifying and announcing, it is urgently ordered that the hospital comply, and to record the order and notify everyone and transfer it to the Lawyers Association of each province for compliance, this order. In this regard, the announcement is urgently notified to everyone.

Zhang Weihan Visited Chiang to Say Goodbye 176

Chiang gave some instructions on the civil affairs of the province of Guizhou Zhang Weihan, the commissioner of the Guizhou Provincial Committee and concurrently the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, came to Beijing in the winter of the 17th year to represent the provincial government to attend the conference on the revision of the Sino-French-Vietnamese Trade Treaty and assisted the foreign king. After more than a year of efforts, the entire treaty has been fully negotiated, but because of the successive changes in the French cabinet, the French ambassador has not yet been instructed to come to Beijing to sign it. Zhang has repeatedly received telegrams from Long Yun, the chairman of the provincial government, urging him to return, and it is difficult to wait any longer. Therefore, he decided to return to Guizhou. Before that, he telegraphed Chairman Chiang to ask for instructions. Chiang replied and ordered him to go to Beijing to meet him before leaving Shanghai. Chiang had left Beijing on a tour, so Zhang was still waiting quietly in Shanghai. It was heard that Chairman Chiang arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou yesterday and summoned Zhang to meet him at the Song residence on Seymour Road at 6:00 p.m. for a long time. He gave some instructions on the affairs of Guizhou province. Zhang has purchased a ticket for a certain company's ship and will leave Shanghai next week to return to Guizhou to take up his new post as the director of the Department of Civil Affairs. He will come to Beijing again to participate in the signing of the treaty when it is scheduled.

Conscription Office Hosted a Farewell Banquet for Chu Minyi Yesterday 180

Lin Kanghou and Wang Xiaolai, directors of the National Government's Conscription Office for the Belgium Exposition, hosted a farewell banquet for Representative Chu Minyi at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday at 3:00 PM. Yu Qiaqing, Ye Huijun, Zhao Jinqing, Gu Xin'yi, Wang Yansong, Sun Fuji, Xu Jiqing, Tu Kaizheng, Shou Jingwei, Chen Yiyan, and more than ninety others attended. Chairman Lin Kanghou gave a farewell speech, in addition to describing the progress of the conscription, he hoped that Representative Chu would promote the spirit and civilization of our country to the outside world during this trip to Belgium, and bring back the material civilization of Europe and the West for research.

In response, Representative Chu, in addition to expressing his gratitude, reported on the goods that had already been shipped in the first and second batches and his opinions on the display after arriving in Belgium. He mainly focused on three categories: education, industry, and agriculture. Wang Yansong then gave a speech detailing the reasons for the recent decline in industry and commerce in our country, which was quite thorough. Tea and refreshments were served, and a group photo was taken in the courtyard to commemorate the event. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Further Records on Chinese Merchants Maintaining Yangtze River Transportation 181

Seagoing Vessels Responding to Emergency After the suspension of 14 Chinese Yangtze River vessels, the local shipping companies were quite anxious, as Shanghai had a large backlog of goods waiting to be shipped out. Currently, only China Merchants' Jiangxin, Jianghua, and Jiangshun can be launched to Shanghai to operate as usual. However, there are many goods and few ships, which is not enough to meet the demand. Yesterday, the China Merchants Bureau's meeting resulted in the temporary use of the Taishun, a seagoing vessel returning from Guangdong, to respond to the emergency. It was decided to dispatch it to the Yangtze River today to load passengers and goods. At the same time, the headquarters was telegraphed to instruct all ports along the way not to hinder the vessel in order to maintain transportation. Ningbo-Shaoxing Purchase of Ships In order to save the Yangtze River navigation rights and resist foreign merchants' monopoly, the Ningbo-Shaoxing Shipping Company specifically entrusted Da Feng Yangxing to purchase 2,400 tons

of steamships from Hong Kong Nuowei shipping companies. This ship was built in 1915, although it is a seagoing vessel, its draft and other aspects are quite suitable for Yangtze River navigation, so it was decided to purchase

it to expand Yangtze River voyages. The ship price is fourteen thousand

pounds, which is equivalent to more than 190,000 Shanghai dollars. It was heard yesterday that the contract has been signed and the transaction has been completed, and the ship will be delivered immediately. The ship's name is "Immed

Love", and it is expected to arrive in Shanghai within a week. After some repairs, it can be dispatched to Shanghai-Hankou. The new ship name has not yet been determined.

Revised Package Price China Merchants Bureau's Yangtze River ships have recently seen an increase in passengers. The bureau plans to increase the passenger package price for each ship. The business section has drafted a proposal to increase the monthly passenger package price for large ships departing on Mondays and Thursdays to 2,800 yuan, and the monthly passenger package price for mid-level ships departing on the 3rd and 6th to 2,700 yuan. In case of minor ship groundings or damage, and transportation of soldiers, etc., with short deadlines, the bureau may, at its discretion, subsidize 15%. In case of damage, suspension of navigation, and other major circumstances, further discussion will be held. A notice has been sent to all business directors yesterday. Zhengzhou Goods Interrupted Every year in April and May, goods from Zhengzhou are extremely crowded, and they are all loaded by the Yangtze River to Shanghai and then transferred to

overseas vessels to European countries. Peanuts, soybeans, cotton and other goods are the best. Recently, due to the changing situation, the arrival of goods from Zhengzhou has been interrupted. Not only has the downstream business of the Yangtze River vessels been sharply reduced, but also the export of European ships has been affected. According to news from foreign shipping companies yesterday, a large number of peanuts and other goods have been blocked and cannot be loaded on ships to the east.

The Ministry-Appointed Students Studying in the United States Arrive in Canada 182

The students studying in the United States appointed by the Central Party Department, who had previously booked tickets and handled all travel procedures through the China Travel Service, set sail from Shanghai on the Changxing Russian Queen liner on February 15. Now the Changxing Company has received a letter from them from the United States on February 28, describing that since leaving Shanghai, they have been warmly received by the staff on board, and they were extremely comfortable and deeply grateful. On the day of arrival, the local government of Jia Bang and the company specially sent commissioners to guide them to participate in the council, museums, and scenic spots in Victoria, and received the official

welcome from the governor and bureau chiefs. A grand welcoming banquet was held in the evening, attended by members of Congress, overseas branches of the Chinese Kuomintang, the Chinese Association, the General Chamber of Commerce, and representatives from various Chinese organizations. The atmosphere was lively and speeches were given, and the evening ended in joy.

It was also heard that the students were extremely satisfied with the trip, and when reporting to the National Government, they planned to suggest that new

students in the future could take the Queen liner of the Changxing Company, which is large and fast, and can save various procedures.

The Commercial Press Employees' Union Protests the Foreign Soldiers' Homicide 183

At about 7 pm on March 30, outside the Chang'e Dance Hall on Tianzhutang Street, foreign sailors stabbed pedestrians with knives, injuring Song Derong, an employee of the Commercial Press, Zhou Fugen, the owner of a Chinese barber shop, and three other unidentified persons. The Commercial Press Employees' Union proposed opinions and methods for handling this case, divided into short-term and long-term solutions, and requested guidance and assistance from various sectors of society to fight together. The following is a transcript of its telegram to the Municipal Party Department: Submitting the plea for a French soldier to commit a wanton murder, harm compatriots, and implore the government to immediately lodge a serious protest to protect the people's lives and maintain national rights. Your Association member Song Derong, Cui Zhiliang, and Shi Huitang were coming from the office on official matters at about 7 pm on March 30, passing by the Chang'e Dance Hall in Tianzhutang Street, when a French sailor suddenly stabbed Song in the left side of his back with a bayonet. Song fainted and fell to the ground. Cui Zhiliang and Shi Huitang, seeing the sailor coming fiercely, were shocked and ran wildly, while whistling and shouting for help. They were finally tracked down and arrested by a Chinese police officer and sent to the Dabai Mingzhong French Police Station for detention. At the same time, two Chinese police officers, No. 392 and No. 496, inspected the scene and sent the injured Song Derong to Renji Hospital for treatment. His injuries were serious. Afterwards, it was learned that a few minutes before Song was stabbed, Zhou Fugen, the owner of a Chinese barber shop (also on Tianzhutang Street), and a certain person A (name unknown) were also stabbed by the sailor. Zhou's injuries were minor (the knife stabbed about an inch deep in his chest and ribs), while the injuries of Person A were the most serious and it is still unknown where he is being treated. At a time when there are loud calls to abolish unequal treaties, foreigners are still using concessions as a shield and extraterritoriality as a guarantee, daring to commit wanton murders in our Chinese territory. It is a disregard for international etiquette, trampling on human rights, people are the knives, and we are the fish. There have been countless compatriots who have groaned and died miserably under the iron hooves of imperialism. Recently, Zhang Xueliang's blood has not yet dried, and the tragedy on Tianzhutang Street has occurred again. This can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? Therefore, we appeal to the government to immediately lodge a serious protest and achieve the following goals: (1) Short-term solutions: There are three direct requirements regarding this case: 1. The French government should apologize to the Chinese government and guarantee that French citizens will not commit similar acts of violence in the future. 2. The sailor who committed the murder should be punished by Chinese law. 3. The damages and reputation of Song Derong, Zhou Fugen, and others should be compensated with 60,000 taels of silver. (2) Long-term solutions: There are two requirements from the principle of safeguarding national sovereignty: 1. Withdraw the naval and ground forces of all countries stationed in China. 2. Additional Surcharges on Merchant Ships 185

Zhejiang Disaster Relief Due to the disaster in Zhejiang last year, it was agreed upon by the provincial authorities and the Relief Committee that all freight and passenger fares on all ships traveling in Zhejiang, regardless of coastal inland rivers, would be subject to a 10% surcharge for disaster relief. It was initially scheduled to take effect on March 15 for a period of one year, but later, at the request of the shipping companies in Shanghai, it was postponed to April 1. All Chinese and foreign merchant ships, gasoline ships, and deck boats will be subject to the surcharge. The donation will be collected by personnel sent by the managing agency at the ship's destination, who will inspect the books and collect the tax according to the amount of business. Those who conceal or fail to report will be severely punished. Due to package confirmation issues, the Shanghai-Ningbo ships in this city are still under negotiation,

so the implementation is slightly later than other ships. Chongming Sand Dam Donation There are a total of six companies operating the Shanghai-Chongming-Haimen ferries. Currently, the Chongming-Haimen waterway must be dredged in order to allow for smooth navigation. The two county chiefs of Chongming and Haimen have agreed that the first step in dredging the river is to start with building a dam, which requires a total of 4,000 yuan. They have discussed with six shipping companies in Shanghai, including Daxing, to recognize and borrow 4,000 yuan for the project. In the future, surcharges will be collected on each ship ticket to repay the loan. The six companies have met several times and agreed to comply.

Hunan Disaster Relief Conference 187

Held at Renji Hall Yesterday

Hunan Province has suffered particularly severe disasters in recent years, surpassing all other provinces. Although the people of the province have made every effort to save themselves, the disaster is too great and their power is too small to cope with it. Moreover, due to the slow pace of external publicity, the outside world is largely unaware of the actual situation of the Hunan disaster. Now, the province has been suffering from years of famine, and the spring famine is particularly urgent. The province has exhausted all resources. As a last resort, they have publicly elected Mr. Shu Jingxiang to go to Beijing and Shanghai to beg for donations. In addition to visiting the chairman of the Relief Committee and various ministries in Beijing and raising a considerable amount of funds, he recently came to Shanghai with fellow villagers from Beijing, including Qiu Ao, Chen Yu, Ma Zhenwu, Shu Chushi, Tang San, etc., to discuss with Xu Junren, chairman of the National Government Relief Committee, and Wang Yiting, Yu Qiaqing, Tan Zuan, Yi Yincun, and the Shanghai gentry from the province, Yu Yaoqu, Wang Songnian, Zeng Nongran, Nie Yuntai, Nie Lusheng, Tan Pingzhai, etc., at the Yunnan Road Renji Hall, and sent invitations to people from all walks of life in Shanghai to gather and raise funds. A total of more than eighty people attended, and Xu Junren was publicly elected as chairman. First, the chairman gave an opening speech, followed by Qiu Ao, who gave a detailed account of the disaster situation and the process of handling relief affairs. It was agreed to publicly elect all the people present as initiators to take charge of raising funds in different ways to benefit the disaster victims, and more than 10,000 yuan was raised on the spot.

Social Affairs Bureau Investigates the Situation of Residents in the City Center 190

Since the municipal government designated a part of the Yinhang and Yinxiang districts under its jurisdiction as the central urban area, it is deeply concerned that the general public does not fully understand it, and decided to start with publicity first. Membership Fee Issue of Trade Associations 191

Each industry can set its own rules. Explanation from the Business Consolidation Council.

Regarding the regulations on membership fees in the articles of association of trade associations, the Business Consolidation Council sent a letter to the Chicken and Duck Trade Association, stating, "In reply, your letter dated the 27th of this month was received, stating that the articles of association of trade associations established by our council do not specify the membership fee, and the maximum amount that can be charged is unknown. Please give instructions to follow." According to Article 12 of the Implementing Rules of the Law on Industrial and Commercial Trade Associations: "The expenses of the association shall be borne by the members, and the method of sharing shall be decided by the members' representatives congress." Therefore, the maximum amount of this membership fee can be determined as appropriate, and then submitted to the members' representatives congress of the association for decision, and then added to the articles of association of the association. The articles of association of trade associations issued by our council are originally common regulations based on the general situation of various industries, for the use of the blueprint of each association. As for the detailed and refined situation, each industry is different, so it may as well be added by itself after discussion and decision." To the Shanghai Special Municipality Chicken and Duck Trade Association.

Sixty-Three-Year-Old Yang Qinxue Kidnapped 193

Returning Home by Chartered Car in the Evening. Sudden Kidnappers Block the Way. The Old Man Was Weak and Could Not Resist. The Bandit's Car Was Rented and Robbed.

Yang Qinxue, from Nanxiang, runs the Yutai Bean and Wheat Shop at No. 63, Fen Lane, Jiuhua Road, Nanshi. At about 7 p.m. last night, he was kidnapped by bandits while returning home from the shop in his own chartered car. The bandits were both holding pistols. Their car was No. 1483, rented from the Weihai Automobile Shop at No. 902, Weihaiwei Road. After tying Yang into the car, they sped away south from Xiaojiuhua Road. The police officer at the post of the First District and Third Precinct Public Security Bureau caught a glimpse of the car number and reported it to the station for investigation.

Old and Weak, Kidnapped into the Car 194

Yang Qinxue is 63 years old this year. He goes to and from the shop twice a day in his own chartered car. The driver, Lu Laowu, has been working for many years. Yesterday morning at about 10 a.m., Lu pulled the car to the Yutai Shop. At about 7 p.m., he left the shop to return home. When he reached Xiaojiuhua Road, suddenly two men came forward and stopped the chartered car. The comers were wearing black robes, about 30 years old, and spoke with a Shanghai accent. One of them was wearing a felt hat. After stopping the car, he said to Yang, "Don't make a sound," and showed him a gun. Because Yang was old and weak, he was unable to resist and let them do what they wanted. One bandit threw down the car pole with force, and Yang was immediately kidnapped and boarded a car that had been parked on the roadside, and sped away. The location of the incident was sparsely populated, and no one noticed it at night. However, the chartered car driver, Lu A'wu, seemed to see a young woman sitting in the bandit's car, perhaps as a disguise. The bandit's car sped away towards Xiaonanmen. Because the speed of the car was abnormal, it was noticed by the police officer at the post of the First District and Third Precinct Public Security Bureau near the Social Affairs Bureau. He caught a glimpse of the number 1483. He wanted to stop it, but it was too late. Like an arrow leaving the bow, he watched it go away.

Bandit's Car Rented and Robbed 195

The car No. 1483 used by the bandits was rented from the Weihai Automobile Shop at No. 902, Weihaiwei Road, in the Public Concession beforehand. At that time, at about 6:50 p.m., a middle-aged man came to the Weihai Automobile Shop, wearing a black robe, a felt hat, and speaking with a local accent. He claimed to be surnamed Zhang and lived at No. 87, Mendland Road. He wanted to rent a car to pick up his mother-in-law for dinner. The accountant ordered the driver, Xi Linfu, to drive the open car No. 1483 to respond to the guest and drive straight to the Great West Road in Huxi. When he reached the intersection of Avenue Joffre, the person in the car suddenly ordered the driver to stop. At that time, an accomplice had been ambushed on the roadside. He took out a gun and forced Xi Linfu to get out of the car. Xi had no way to resist and obeyed. The bandits jumped into the car and drove away. The driver went to a Westerner's house at No. 7, Avenue Joffre, to borrow a telephone to notify the car shop, and reported to the Jing'an Temple Police Station. Western and Chinese detectives were immediately dispatched to investigate in all directions. After the bandits robbed the car, they drove to Nanshi and kidnapped Yang Qinxue.

Gunfire Rains on Xinzha Road, Fierce Battle to Capture Bandits 196

Special Team Checks Pedestrians. A Bandit Opens Fire. Japanese Detective Short Stature, Lucky to Survive. In the Pool of Blood, the Thug Loses His Life. At 7:30 p.m. last night, between Xinzha Road and Carter Road, two Japanese patrol officers and two Chinese patrol officers from the Gordon Road Police Station departed to check pedestrians. A man, about 30 years old, wearing a black robe and a copper basin hat, was told to retreat. The Japanese patrol officer of the team thought that the car was too close and wanted to go back, and that the person in the car looked flustered, knowing that he was not a good person, so he went forward to check. Unexpectedly, as soon as the Japanese officer approached him, the man took out a pistol from his sleeve and shot the officer in the chest. Fortunately, the Japanese officer had a bulletproof vest, so the bullet flew over and sparks burst. The officer immediately fought back, but also missed. At this time, the patrol officer who came to check with him saw that the bandit was so bold and immediately went forward to help capture him. The bandit opened fire on the Japanese officer again. Because the Japanese officer was short, the bullet grazed his shoulder. The four patrol officers had no choice but to take out their guns and shoot the bandit head-on. For a time, gunfire rained down and pedestrians disappeared. The bandit retreated while firing. The patrol officers tried their best to chase forward. Later, because the bandit's bullets were exhausted, he fled to the corner of the Xinzha Road Small Vegetable Market, onto the door of the Xinchang Electric Material Shop, and was shot in the shoulder by the patrol officers. The bullet passed through and blood flowed profusely. Still wanting to muster his remaining courage, he fled west. The Japanese officer fired another shot, hitting the bandit in the waist. The bullet entered the abdomen and he immediately fell to the ground. After a while, he died. Later, the police officer at the post telegraphed the police station in charge and dispatched two police cars to search the surrounding alleys for accomplices. As a result, nothing was found. The body was transported to the Filun Road Coroner's Office for an autopsy. It is scheduled to be autopsied this morning.

Police Officer Kang Zhendong Describes the Circumstances of the Madman's Murder 199

Woman Died After Hearing the Alarm. Shooting a Little Later, the Child Would Not Have Survived.

The case of the madman Zhang Jiazhen killing a woman and a child with a knife on Zhonghua Road outside Xiaonanmen has been reported three times in this newspaper. It is now learned that prosecutor Yang of the local court, in order to understand the facts of the case and whether it was true madness, in addition to going to the hospital to ask for a detailed confession, yesterday summoned Kang Zhendong, the police officer at the Xiaozha Bridge Police Station of the First District and Third Precinct, who arrested Zhang Jiazhen at the time, to the case for preliminary hearing. When asked about the situation at the time, Kang replied, "At about 1 p.m., I was on duty in front of the Social Affairs Bureau and saw two women passing by with panicked expressions. When I asked them, they said that someone was killing people on the road. I loaded my gun and moved forward and saw a person holding a knife and killing a big child. At that time, Wu Zhou had already died. I shouted, but he was not afraid, so I fired a shot into the sky, but he was still not afraid, and the second knife was already down. Seeing the urgency of the situation, I fired a shot at his leg, hitting his left leg. Unexpectedly, he did not feel any pain, and the third knife was already down, and the child died. He then held a knife and killed a younger child. The child dodged and injured the child's hand. I fired another shot and hit his right foot. Unexpectedly, after being hit, he turned around and saw me, and then held a knife to kill me. I had no choice but to fire another shot, hitting his abdomen, and he fell to the ground." The official asked, "Do you know how to kill the woman?" He replied, "Afterwards, I heard people say that the madman was dancing wildly on the road with a knife and bumped into the woman. The woman scolded him for bumping into people, and the madman killed the woman." Asked, "How did the patrol officer Li Jieshan get injured?" He replied, "Because he heard the gunshot and came to help me, he was hit in the foot by a stray bullet, but it did not hinder him." Asked, "What did he say when he was arrested?" He replied, "When I saw the madman fall and arrested him, I asked him why he killed people. He said that God told me to kill, for the sake of inequality, and said, 'Quickly kill me, I have already killed people.'" The official asked, "If you were faster, you could have saved one of the children who was killed." He replied, "I couldn't be faster. If I was a little slower, another child would have died." After Yang recorded the confession, he ordered him to leave, and after the madman recovered, he would submit a proposal for interrogation again.

Poor Chinese. Ancient Morality is Admirable.

Grain Exchange Increases Security Deposit 204

Hidden to Limit Speculation. In the Shanghai rice market, japonica rice has always been the most numerous in sales, and foreign indica rice has very little sales. However, recently, rice prices have gradually increased. The price of high-quality japonica rice has increased to as much as 20 yuan. The source is not large. Fortunately, foreign rice is used for sales, but the price is also gradually increasing. Generally, speculators take advantage of the current spring season, and the market price is rising step by step. If it reaches the summer season, when the old and new crops are not yet harvested, the price will definitely increase again, so they are buying up in the market, especially futures, resulting in limited spot foreign rice transactions in the market recently, and futures exceeding spot by several times. Last week, the price of japonica rice soared to 21 yuan, causing panic. Foreign rice transactions are unusually prosperous. The market transactions are all futures, with 60,000 to 70,000 or 40,000 to 50,000 transactions per day. Therefore, the market is becoming more and more urgent. It is heard that people outside the industry have also inserted themselves into the operation. The Chinese Grain Association, due to the increasingly rising market, which is detrimental to people's food, Chairman Ye Huijun and other leaders discussed and decided that, in order to protect the credit of the industry, from

Page 16

April 1, the buyer and seller of foreign rice futures transactions each pay a security deposit of 1,000 taels per 100 tons to consolidate. After this method was determined, the trading of foreign rice futures in the market on the day before yesterday suddenly became clear. It is necessary to have a security deposit before buying and selling, so the general brokers are preparing to sell the previously booked futures rice, so the market is slightly stagnant. It is also heard that the price of foreign rice privately operated by industry colleagues and friends was previously marked with a seal. Now, each line manager has cracked down on it and issued a bulletin stating that if any friends in the line privately operate foreign rice without entering the accounts, the line will not be responsible, and the friends will be responsible for solving it themselves. It is thought that the market will not be firm and tight again in the future.

Verdict in the Case of Firearms Hidden in Cement Pillars 207

Han Changmao Sentenced to Two Months' Imprisonment. Firearms were hidden in cement pillars in the warehouse of Guanji Coal Shop, Dongyouheng Road. On the 23rd of last month, a pillar cracked, revealing a Mauser pistol and bullets. The shop owner, Han Changmao, transferred it to a pile of bricks. The Harbin Police Station searched and seized it, and detained the shop owner and the stacker Li Changsheng, as well as the rickshaw puller Wang Sanzi, who had been a detective Yao A'sheng before he was removed from office, and sent them to the Provisional Court. According to Han's confession, the stone pillar was deposited by Yao in the past. Judge Xu instructed to adjourn the hearing. As reported earlier, Judge Xu continued the hearing again yesterday afternoon. First, the Chinese and Western detectives reported that they had broken all the remaining cement pillars and checked them and found no firearms. Then, Han Changmao's brother, Han Changshan, testified that the stone pillars were deposited by Yao A'sheng in the first month of the previous year, who asked someone to bring them by car. At that time, he only said that they would be stored temporarily for two or three days, and he did not know that firearms were hidden inside. He had never come to pick them up. The defendant Li Changsheng confessed that the pillar in which firearms were found was ordered to be broken by Han Changmao. Wang Sanzi confessed that Yao A'sheng ordered him to send the nine stone pillars to the coal shop for deposit. At that time, Yao was still a detective, so I was inconvenient to report it. Han Changmao's confession was vague, and he hired a lawyer to defend him. After the interrogation, Judge Xu sentenced Han Changmao to two months' imprisonment and confiscated the firearms.

Li and Wang were acquitted. Chief Prosecutor Zhou Xianjue also attended the court and sat with Judge Xu to perform his prosecutorial duties during the trial.

The Detective Squad Leader Position Following Qiao Songsheng's Death 210

Director Yuan Has Selected Someone

Municipal Public Security Bureau Director Yuan has been considering candidates for the detective squad leader position vacated by Qiao Songsheng's illness and death. In recent days, recommendations for the position have flooded in from various quarters. Yesterday, someone inquired about the situation, and Director Yuan stated that Squad Leader Qiao had served him for ten months, solving numerous major cases and proving a valuable assistant. His unfortunate demise is deeply regrettable. In recent days, recommendation letters for the squad leader position have arrived in an almost blizzard-like fashion, which he found rather pointless. It should be known that the position of squad leader is of utmost importance to the security of this city, and only someone with excellent academic qualifications, experience, and character can fill it. He has already selected someone and is in the process of submitting the request. Until the approval is granted, Deputy Squad Leader Lu will continue to act as temporary agent.

Extension of the Second Phase of Industrial and Commercial Registration 211

Deadline is April 30th

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs has been processing the second phase of industrial and commercial registration since February 1st, originally limited to two months, ending on March 31st. It is now heard that industries such as South Goods and Coal, due to the hurried timeframe, were unable to complete the registration within the deadline. Representatives were sent to the Bureau to earnestly request an extension. After investigation, the Bureau found that the respective trade associations are in the process of reorganization, and therefore granted a one-month extension, with the deadline now set for April 30th. All households belonging to industries included in the second phase of registration, such as bathhouses, barbershops, quail farms, South Goods businesses, Western clothing tailors, bookstores, cloth merchants, etc., that have not yet registered, may also request registration with the Bureau. No further extensions will be granted after the deadline. It is also heard that for those in the first phase of registration such as old goods businesses, sauce gardens, coal businesses, printing businesses, silk and satin businesses, weights and measures businesses, etc., a small number of those who have exceeded the deadline, the Bureau has already sent letters to the Public Security Bureau to instruct the district offices to punish them in accordance with Article 8 of the Industrial and Commercial Registration Regulations, and to order them to register.

The Municipal Government has approved the communication from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce stating that the deadline for the verification and renewal of business licenses for exchange brokers has passed. All business licenses for brokers issued by the former Beijing Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce and Ministry of Industry that have not been verified must be re-submitted for approval and registration before they can serve as brokers. Anonymous Letter Leads to the Discovery of Runaway Wife 213

Enticed by a Relative of the Second Landlord

Wife Claims Husband's Family is Penniless

Zhang, the wife of Dong Liangming, a Ningbo native residing at No. 434 Beiler Road in the French Concession, secretly ran away on February 12th of this year, disappearing without a trace. Dong searched everywhere without success, until recently, when Dong received an anonymous letter stating that his wife had been abducted by Xi A-wu, a relative of the second landlord. Dong immediately took the letter to the police station, ordering detectives to go to Pudong, where they apprehended Xi and Zhang and brought them back to the police station. Yesterday, they were brought to the French court for investigation. The plaintiff first presented the previous events and hired a lawyer who stated that the defendant, Xi A-wu, had committed the crime of enticement and requested that he be punished according to law and that the embezzled sum of 240 yuan and clothing be recovered. Xi confessed that Zhang had been frequently beaten by her husband, so she went out and asked people to escort her to her relative's home, and he did not dare to entice her. Zhang's confession was similar, and she also stated that her husband was very poor, his family being penniless. How could there be silver dollars and clothing embezzled? She requested an investigation. The judge ordered the two defendants to post bail and await further investigation.

Female Abductor Awaiting Transfer after Public Security Bureau Issues Official Document 214

The Sixth District Public Security Bureau of Shanghai West recently apprehended a female abductor named Wu Ma-shi. According to her confession, on January 22nd, she enticed Shi Ding-shi's nine-year-old daughter, A-mei, and sold her to Chen Lu-shi, a resident of No. 112 Wuding Road, for 400 yuan. Yesterday, they were brought to the Special District Local Court for investigation. Patrol leader Wang presented an official letter requesting a transfer. However, the police lawyer Ru Bao-yi appeared in court and stated that for all cases transferred by mainland authorities, according to the precedent during the Provisional Court era, an official document from the local court or the Municipal Public Security Bureau under the Municipal Government must be submitted to the court before the transfer is approved. Today, the Sixth District only has a letter, which does not seem serious enough. Chen Lu-shi also hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend her. Judge Feng instructed the defendant to be detained pending the official document from the court, while Chunlan was temporarily detained at the Jiliang Institute.

Beggar Chases After Car for Money 215

Fatally Crushed by the Car

Yang Ji-tang, a beggar from Shandong, had a nine-year-old daughter named He-er who followed in his footsteps, begging for money from passersby on Kangqu Road in southern Shanghai. Recently, with many people visiting Longhua, the beggars saw it as a good opportunity, chasing after and running regardless of the dangers in the road. At 5 p.m. the day before yesterday, a car returning from Longhua sped past, knocking He-er down and crushing her skull, killing her instantly. The driver sped away, leaving the victim with no way to seek justice. Yesterday, the Fifteenth Ward's Baozhang (local security officer) Gu Zhonglian reported the incident to the local court. Inspector Li and others confirmed the death and ordered the body to be collected.

Cause of Bian Zhaojin's Death Unclear 216

Requires Autopsy by a Western Doctor

The case of Bian Zhaojin, the owner of a rosewood workshop at No. 1, Lane 29, Tianzhutang Street, South City Xinpu Yutang, who died after being beaten by his nephew Bian Wan, has been reported yesterday. It is now known that the case originated when Bian Linwan owed Bian Zhaojin more than 20 yuan. Bian Zhaojin demanded repayment, and Bian Linwan agreed to pay 5 yuan first, promising to pay on the date before that, but the money was not forthcoming and a fight broke out. The next day, after Bian Zhaojin died, Bian Linwan went into hiding. The deceased's family then went to the Second District Second Precinct to accuse him, saying that there was also an accomplice named Huang Siyuan. So the precinct first arrested Huang Siyuan. Huang Siyuan's wife, in desperation, found Bian Linwan yesterday morning and dragged him to the precinct. They were transferred to the local court for pretrial by Inspector Li. The defendants claimed that they did not beat the deceased, and that the deceased had committed suicide by swallowing opium. But the daughter of the deceased, Bian Xiaoyun, said that her father was a member of the rationalist sect and did not use tobacco or alcohol, and that he was beaten to death. The official instructed that the defendants be detained temporarily and went to the scene to inspect the body for a long time. It was difficult to determine how he died, so he ordered the body to be taken to the court. In the afternoon, forensic doctor Liu Nan-qun performed an autopsy. At the time, he could not immediately determine the cause of death, and said that he would bring the viscera to the court for testing and then report. The body was collected by the family.

Steam Car Emits Sparks 217

Burning Down Six Grass Houses by the Roadside

The official operation of steam-powered automobiles on the Songhu Branch Road has been reported in this newspaper. However, the chimney of the car emits a lot of sparks, which is inconvenient for passengers on the platform and pedestrians by the roadside. Yesterday, the wind was strong. When the car was running, sparks from the chimney were continuously emitted like flying flowers. At about 9:00 a.m., when passing Zhanghuabang Station, sparks landed on the Chen family's thatched house by the roadside, igniting it instantly, spreading to the neighboring houses, and becoming a raging fire. The Wusong fire brigades were alerted. Because the road was narrow, they could not get to the scene to put out the fire. In less than half an hour, all six thatched houses were reduced to ashes.

Guangming Printing House Temporarily Sealed 218

Printing Reactionary Newspapers

Five Workers Arrested

Recently, reactionary publications have been found in the market, and although their sale has been banned and news vendors arrested and punished, the printing location is very secret, making it difficult to eradicate the source. To prevent such reactionary publications from appearing again, the concession authorities have ordered all police stations to pay attention and crack down on printing houses and prohibit printing. It has now been discovered that the "Hai Guang Daily" and "Dong Fang Bao", two newspapers whose publication is prohibited, are printed by the Guangming Printing House on Parker Road. At 9:00 a.m. the day before yesterday, detective Zhou Guisheng from the Xinzha police station, along with Western detective chief Huai Tuo, went to the printing house and confiscated 1,000 copies each of the two reactionary newspapers and arrested five printing workers: Wang Desheng, Jin Zhusheng, Qian Tianbao, Ji Genquan, Cheng Agui. Yesterday, they were taken to the Special District Local Court. Lawyer Ru Bao-yi represented the police in prosecuting them and requested punishment according to Article 160 of the Criminal Law. The detectives testified that when they went to search the premises, Wang Desheng was proofreading, and the other four were printing. When questioned, Wang Desheng gave evasive answers, claiming that he was visiting a friend at the printing house. The other four defendants admitted that they were workers at the printing house, which was owned by a person with the surname Yu. The newspapers were brought in by Yu for printing. Wang Desheng had come to the printing house to collect them yesterday. Judge Feng ordered the defendants to be detained and rescheduled the hearing. The Guangming Printing House was temporarily sealed, and the police were ordered to seize its books and present them to the court.

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Issues Free and Half-Price Passes for the Pujiang Ferry 219

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities operates the Pujiang Ferry. In order to provide preferential treatment to various municipal agencies traveling to and from the Pujiang River, it previously issued a type of free pass and stipulated regulations, which have been revised and disclosed in the newspapers. Recently, the Bureau, considering the Municipal Ferry as a municipal business, and in order to strive for progress, has strictly limited the issuance of free passes and added a type of half-price pass. It has also drafted regulations for the issuance of free and half-price passes for the Pujiang Ferry, which have been submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and promulgation. The regulations are summarized as follows: (1) To apply for free or half-price passes for the Pujiang Ferry, you must first apply to the Municipal Government for approval, which will then notify the Bureau of Public Utilities to issue the passes. (2) Free passes will only be issued to the following agencies that need to send people to travel between the east and west banks of the Pujiang River on the Pujiang Ferry from time to time: (A) All bureaus and districts under this Municipal Government (bureaus and districts are limited to those within the ferry line range), (B) Other agencies that use municipal funds. (Type A) Non-transferrable pass will be issued, and the bearer must present the employee ID issued by the service agency when using it. (Type B) Registered passes will be issued, and the agency must designate two representatives, attach recent two-inch half-length photos, and fill in their positions. (3) Half-price passes will be issued to the following agencies that need to send people to travel between the east and west banks of the Pujiang River on the Pujiang Ferry from time to time: (A) All Party, government, and military agencies in the city, (B) Agencies related to the ferry. Registered passes will be issued, and a recent two-inch half-length photo must be attached and the position filled in. (4) Free or half-price passes are limited to two per agency. In special circumstances, the Municipal Government may grant a special increase, but not more than two. (5) If the users of registered free or half-price passes change, the agency should send the free or half-price pass to the Bureau of Public Utilities to apply for a new pass. (6) Free or half-price passes are valid for one year, but within fifteen days of the start of each quarter, the pass holder must send the pass to the Bureau of Public Utilities to stamp it as proof. (7) Holders of free passes must comply with the ferry regulations and pay attention to the following: (A) The free pass is only allowed for personal use on official business and may not be used by others, (B) Only second-class seats are allowed. If you want to sit in a special or first-class seat, you must pay the difference, (C) Each free pass is limited to one person. A separate cargo ticket must be purchased for carrying goods, (D) The free pass must be handed over when checked. If any of the above items are violated, the Bureau of Public Utilities may cancel the free pass. (8) Holders of half-price passes should first purchase tickets at the ticket office with the pass before boarding, and abide by the ferry regulations. If you make up for the ticket after sailing, you must pay the original price. (9) If a free or half-price pass is lost, the agency may prove it and apply to the Bureau of Public Utilities for a replacement, but unregistered passes should first be declared invalid in the newspaper and the original advertisement sent to the Bureau of Public Utilities for record. (10) When the reason for issuing a free or half-price pass ceases to exist, the Bureau of Public Utilities may report the pass to the Municipal Government for cancellation. (11) These measures are approved and implemented by the Shanghai Special Municipal Government. Note: Free and half-price passes should be equipped with a cornered envelope, and each copy costs 30 cents in silver.

Reform of the Songhu Jiaoyangyuan (Reformatory) 220

Wang Zhaocheng, the supervising director of the Songhu Jiaoyangyuan, since taking over as the director of the institute, arrives at the institute every morning at 10:00 a.m. and goes to the office set up in the Shangzhenghui (Association for the Promotion of Commerce and Government) at 5:00 p.m. to supervise the staff. Wu Wenhua and Others Survey Yutang Yesterday 221

Yesterday (2nd) at 10:00 a.m., Wu Wenhua, Director of the County Construction Bureau, along with Yang Fulin, head of the Third District, Peng Liren, head of the Second District, and more than ten local gentry including Peng Yinqiao, Sun Shiben, Chen Danian, Ni Binzhi, and Jiang Shijie, surveyed Yutang. Starting from the Huangpu River and heading west along Yutang, passing Tangwan and reaching Beiqiao, they traveled fifteen or sixteen li in total. It is planned that tomorrow they will go from Beiqiao, passing Machiao and directly reaching the lower reaches, Yuerjing. The situation of yesterday's survey is recorded below: (1) From the entrance of Huangpu to Yutang Bridge, it is about one mile. The river channel can still pass through smoothly, and there is no need to dredge this section. However, the riverbed from Yutang Bridge, Tangwan Town to Beiqiao is very silted. According to the old dredging precedent, the river surface is four zhang. But for future transportation, it is not enough to widen the river surface to five or six zhang. This matter is of great importance, and will be discussed at the meeting to be taken seriously. (2) From near Yutang Bridge, the river suddenly turns north to Xinmu Bridge, which is about two miles long and forms an arc, commonly known as Be灣 (North Bay). Also to the east of Xinmu Bridge and west of Yutang Bridge, there is a Jinjia River, about half a li long, which goes east to Yutang and west to Xinmu Bridge, like a diameter. It is suggested that the Yutang Bridge section be filled in and used as public property, and that the river be changed to come out of Yutang through Jinjia River, which will not affect farmland water conservancy and will save a lot of effort in engineering. This matter also needs to be discussed at the meeting. (3) From Huangpu westward along Yutang, passing Tangwan Town and reaching Beiqiao, there are a total of six large and small bridges. Among them, four can still be used, but two wooden bridges are in disrepair and dangerous for pedestrians. It is necessary to know how to repair or rebuild them, which can be determined according to the budget in the future.

Handling the Issue of Company Public Reserve Fund 222

The Accountants Association Submits an Explanation to the Ministry

The Shanghai Accountants Association, based on a letter from member Jin Zongcheng, a CPA, requesting an explanation of whether the company's public reserve fund is the right of shareholders or whether labor can also share in the profits, stated that the matter concerns laws and regulations and cannot be arbitrarily discussed from a theoretical perspective. It submitted a document to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce stating that it was submitting for instruction regarding the handling of the company's public reserve fund and earnestly requested that it be forwarded for interpretation. The matter was reported by the member Jin Zongcheng stating that a company has a total capital of 50,000 yuan and a public reserve fund of more than 100,000 yuan. Now the shareholders propose to increase the capital, that is, to distribute the public reserve fund to the shareholders as shares, but the labor force opposes it, thinking that the public reserve fund is the public reserve of the company and that the labor force should also share in the profits. According to commercial practice, at the end of each accounting period, all profits, in addition to the public reserve fund, are also used to pay bonuses to the labor force. Where do these flowers come from? In fact, it is the same nature as the public reserve fund, and it is income distributed under the profit item. However, whether this public reserve fund can be shared by labor is not clearly stipulated in commercial law. In order to seek a solution and have something to follow, a special letter is sent for inquiry and it is requested that it be put forward for discussion at the meeting. Based on this, after discussion at the association meeting, it was determined that the matter concerns laws and regulations and cannot be arbitrarily discussed from a theoretical perspective. It is appropriate to submit the letter from the member containing the various sections to the Ministry, earnestly requesting that it be forwarded to the judicial authorities for interpretation and reply, so that there may be compliance. It is now heard that the association has received a reply from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Shangzi No. 9089, which states that the report has been received and the situation has been reported to the Executive Yuan for forwarding for interpretation. Further instructions should await arrival at the Ministry before verification.

Shangzhenghui Reports on the Process of Reorganizing the Silk and Satin Industry 223

The Shangzhenghui reported to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce on the process of reorganizing the silk and satin industry groups. The case was based on recent reports that the Shanghai Shandong Henan Silk Industry Association, the Zhehu Crepe Industry Association, the Hang Silk Industry Qianjiang Guild Hall, the Su Satin Industry Xuejin Association, etc., had submitted a document to the Ministry stating that the association was forcibly merging existing organizations with completely different business natures and requested relief. The Shangzhenghui could have remained silent before the Ministry instructed the Shangzhenghui to restore order after consulting with the various Gongsuo, but in order to expedite the progress of the Shangzhenghui's reorganization of the silk and satin industry groups, the Shangzhenghui, lest the misunderstanding of this industry should hinder the reorganization process, would have no small impact on the reorganisation plan, so the Shangzhenghui had made a detailed statement to the Ministry, stating the misunderstandings and misinterpretations of the industry, in the hope that the misunderstandings would be quickly corrected, and not to be repetitive. In order to facilitate public convenience, it is hereby announced that the reorganisation of commercial organisations by the Association is carried out in accordance with the powers conferred by the central government's formulation of the organisational outline, and the standard for the reorganisation is based entirely on the Law of the Industrial and Commercial Association promulgated by the National Government, and the procedure for the reorganisation and organisation of the Industrial and Commercial Association drafted by the Association has also been submitted to the Central Party Department and the Ministry for separate filing, except that the first and second articles of the procedure have been approved by the Central Party Department and were deemed to be illegal, The rest of the articles have been regarded as supplementary provisions to the Law of the Industrial and Commercial Association and its Implementing Rules, and do not conflict with the laws and regulations, and the original complaint that the provisions of the articles are in fact intended to be enforced is in fact contrary to the provisions of Article 14 of the Law of the Industrial and Commercial Association, which requires that those whose purposes are in accordance with the provisions of Article 2 of this Law be ordered to reorganise themselves at regular intervals, and that they still have to meet the requirements of Article 3, which states that there shall be one association in one area, and this principle is clear and cannot be disregarded, the Gongsuos are also aware that it cannot be denied on this point, and therefore strongly assert that the Gongsuos have no other completely identical organisations in the city, and that the term 'same industry' in Article 3 of the Law of the Industrial and Commercial Association, in short, means that the business is the same, The Gongsuos are engaged in the sale of silk and satin, although there is a classification of silk crepe yarns and government silk among them, just as the tea sold by the tea industry has products from various provinces such as Hunan, Hubei, Zhejiang, and Anhui, and the detailed differences in the names of their tea, which fill up pages, are just like the classification of silk crepe yarns and government silk, and so is the rice industry and other industries, to give just the above two examples, then the same tea and the same rice, the source of the goods is different, the selling price is different, the cost is different, the freight is different, the sales are different, and the taxation is different, the eight points raised by the Gongsuo in its original submission are almost all similar, if so, apart from tea shops and tea warehouses, rice shops and rice shops, the differences in the eight points are almost all similar, and if so, apart from tea shops and tea warehouses, and rice shops and rice shops, because of the different businesses, there are separate organisations, and the rest have not heard of the classification of goods, which means that they are not completely the same industry and cannot have the same organisation, that the different points raised by the Gongsuos are the sole reason for the silk and satin industry and their persistence in opposing it is because the Gongsuos have had separate organisations in history, and that they cannot be compared to the tea industry and others, even though they have different places of origin and categories, but the so-called different businesses by the Gongsuos are not really different businesses, but are due to different gangs, and that they want to preserve their historical position, whether different gangs in the same industry are allowed to form separate organisations, As an exception to Article 5 of the Law of Industrial and Commercial Associations, although there is no explicit provision, Article 4 of the Association's Procedures for Reorganisation and Organisation was enacted in the interest of the commercial situation, with the proviso that "if there are any customs or business practices that are not possible to merge, they may be varied at the discretion of the Association after verification", which was subsequently approved by the Central Government as being illegal and ordered to be deleted immediately, and the words "habitual history" etc. have been deleted in compliance with the order, and a separate document has been submitted to the Council for the record, so that the organisation with the same business but different gangs and histories must be merged in accordance with the law, as instructed by the Central Government, the Association acts in accordance with the law, and dares not go beyond the scope, and it is unjustifiable for the Gongsuos to claim that they have been suppressed and coerced, and that they have been given an account of the facts based on the original reports published by the Gongsuos, and we respectfully request that the facts be judged and that they be followed for the convenience of the public, and it is also heard that the Council has sent a separate letter to the Municipal Party Department and the Bureau of Social Affairs, setting out the above-mentioned situation.

News from Various Labor Unions 232

Commerce Press Workers' Union: A declaration demanding that the company provide rice subsidies states that the company has been increasingly hardening its stance towards us workers for the past year. We can say with certainty that it is relying on evil forces to restore its position from before the fourteenth year of the Republic and intensify its oppression. We, as oppressed and suffering workers, are now facing an extraordinary rise in rice prices, and we, along with our parents, wives, and children, are finding it extremely difficult to survive in this half-starved state. Therefore, we request the company to find a way to provide relief. However, the company authorities, wearing a mask of culture, are heartlessly harming us and only know how to enrich themselves. They are unwilling to show any sympathy for our plight and have severely rejected our extremely small hope of getting enough to eat. Now that we have reached this point, what else can we say? The meal allowance for employees at the distribution office has already been increased by two yuan, and this money is also provided by the company. Don't the workers at our printing press need to eat? To be honest, this action of ours is not only to solve the immediate problem of rice subsidies, but also to issue a major warning to these cunning capitalists who absolutely cannot be sincerely cooperative with us. If we give in this time, not only will we have no room to speak in the future, but the company will probably make further advances and re-exploit the small amount of benefits we have already obtained. When we think of the history of past struggles and the blood of many martyrs, how can we easily abandon it? How can we be willing to return to a life of slavery? Of course, we are absolutely unwilling. Therefore, we have made a great determination to fight them to the death. We are willing to endure all pain and suffering, even at the cost of our lives. Our vision is already very clear that without considerable sacrifice, we cannot obtain considerable compensation. We are in this dark and depressing state of groaning, and the capitalists are engaged in an offensive plan. To fight for a glimmer of hope, only united solidarity and forward struggle will lead to the final victory, which of course belongs to us.
