Free Talk

One Man's Views 234

— Yang Jia Yi

A woman's authority is exercised only when she cries, because at that moment even the most arrogant man is subdued by her.

Only those who are content can truly enjoy happiness. Otherwise, you may be a wealthy man but live in sorrow every day.

Young friends, you treat your lovers with all your heart, fearing that you are not attentive enough. But you treat your wives only with perfunctory gestures.

If you want to know how strong or weak a man is at a large gathering, just ask if he is afraid of his wife. That will tell you everything.

Don't underestimate the daily cost of cigarettes and tea. If you can save up the money you spend on cigarettes and tea every day, you can provide food for someone for several months.

When a great man wears cloth clothes and walks on two legs, people say he is thrifty. When an ordinary person wears cloth clothes and walks on two legs, people say he is poor.

The words of a bachelor are the lamentations of someone who has lost in love.

The happiness of a marriage based on love is the most difficult to maintain.

The more intelligent you are, the easier it is to be troubled. The more foolish you are, the harder it is to be troubled.

A person who values reputation too much often acts in a way that stains that reputation.

Hen Transformed into Rooster 235

— Fei Gong Zhi

Recently, a family surnamed Wang in the West Market and a family surnamed Hu in the Former Port both had roosters laying eggs. This reminded me that I personally witnessed a hen transforming into a rooster last year. Therefore, I am recording this for those who are curious and want to talk about it. In the North Market of Zhouzhuang Township, Wuxian County, at the home of a Chen family five or six houses away from where I live, several chickens are raised. They are always released to feed in the vacant land behind the house every morning. This is a daily routine. One day, a hen inexplicably transformed into a rooster. It would crow in the middle of the day. Later, it was seen by neighbors, and it was immediately spread as a strange event. I heard about it and went to see it. I waited until noon, and the crowing did occur. I also saw it chasing the other hens and mating with them. As for its appearance, the comb, wattle, and tail feathers gradually increased. Its behavior completely lost its feminine demeanor. People said that the change in domestic animals was a bad omen. The Chen family was deceived by these unfounded rumors and chopped off its head and cooked it. This happened in early May of the 18th year of the Republic.

According to historical records, the transformation of a hen into a rooster does happen occasionally and is not uncommon. But I have never witnessed it before. For example, in the first year of Huanglong during the reign of Emperor Xuan of the Han Dynasty, a hen in the Luling car in the Weiyang Palace transformed into a rooster. In the reign of Emperor Yuan, during the Chuyuan period, in the home of the historian in the Prime Minister's Office, a hen incubating eggs gradually transformed into a rooster. In the first year of Guanghe during the reign of Emperor Ling, a hen in the Southern Palace Servant Temple transformed into a rooster. In the second year of Jingchu during the reign of Emperor Ming of the Wei Dynasty, a hen in the courtyard of the imperial court transformed into a rooster. During the reign of Emperor Yuan of the Jin Dynasty, in Taixing, when Wang Dun was stationed in Wuchang, a hen transformed into a rooster. In August of the first year of Long'an during the reign of Emperor An, in the home of Wang Daozi of Langya, a black hen transformed into a red rooster. In the second year of Yuanxing during the reign of Emperor An, a hen in Hengyang transformed into a rooster. These are only cases where the frontier officials reported the anomalies to the court, and the historians recorded them. How many more cases were scattered in remote villages and fields that were not reported? It can be seen that chickens are the easiest birds to transform, and no other birds have been known to transform. The body constitution may be the reason. In scientific terms, since the discovery of endocrinology by medical scientists, it is known that the human body contains various secretory substances, each with unique properties, which have a chemical association with the products of other organs in the body. That is, there is a chemical interaction in the body. As for the formation and change of sex, it is controlled by the gonads (Keimdrisen). Therefore, it can be changed by artificial addition, subtraction, or replacement. Once replaced, it not only affects the surface, but also the bones, organs, properties, and sounds all change. In 1849, Berthold performed a testicular transplant experiment on chickens, which was able to restore the castrated chicken to its original state. The comb, wattle, feathers, crowing, mating, and all other characteristics of a rooster were fully restored. Decades later, Steinach experimented by exchanging the gonads of male and female animals, which could make the female male and the male female. For example, a female chicken can grow a comb, wattle, change its feathers, crow, and start mating. Mice or rabbits, after gonad transplantation, will change their weak bones, soft fur, full fat, large nipples, and the inherent sexual characteristics of females. When males see them, they will raise their tails and chase them. The mammary glands secrete milk and breastfeed their young. The reason for this obvious and amazing result is the existence of a kind of awakening hormone called Hormon. In social terms, to prove its reason in simple and easy-to-understand terms, the ancient technique of castrating chickens can be pondered and understood. More than half of the problem will be solved.

Record of Cheng Yushuang Learning Swordplay 236

— Romantic Scholar

Cheng Yushuang (Yanqiu) stopped performing at the Xinxin Theater because she was getting fatter. Some said that she would never return to the stage. Those who hoped she would make a name for herself felt sorry for her. But a guest from Tianjin said that Cheng was performing at the Xinxin Grand Theater in Tianjin. Not only was her figure not too bloated, but her singing had reached a higher level. In particular, her performance in the drama "The Story of Red Whiskers" actually incorporated real swordplay, and she danced with a sword on the stage. The reason for this was that Cheng had been learning martial arts from a teacher. I am recording the guest's words to inform those who care about Yushuang's affairs.

Previously, Yushuang was introduced by the owner of Chunming Hall to learn from the boxing master Han. Later, she had to stop because she was busy. Later, as she got fatter and more sluggish, someone suggested that she learn Tai Chi. Yushuang thought it was a good idea and resumed learning from Gao Ziyun. Gao is a famous martial arts master from the north. He used to be the captain of Cao Kunshan's bodyguard. Recently, he has given up fame and devoted himself to teaching. After Yushuang became his student, he loved her for her intelligence and love of learning, and taught her all his skills. Yushuang was also very focused on her studies. In less than three months, she mastered the Qiankun sword. Yushuang said that she was very interested in swordplay. She had once joined a temporary performance at the Beijing YMCA and won the praise of many people. This further encouraged her ambition. This time, when she performed in Tianjin, she extracted the essence of swordplay and incorporated it into her performance. The sword dance scene was therefore transformed into a masterpiece. It was very different from ordinary performers of the drama. Not only did laymen find it colorful and exciting, but even martial arts experts praised it.

Interesting Tidbits from Songjiang 237

— Zhu Si Zhong

(1) Old Shoes Ascend to Heaven

The only means of transportation in Songjiang has always been sedan chairs. The word "sedan chair" sounds like "old shoes" in the mouths of Songjiang people. In the years when sedan chairs were popular, you could often hear the sound of "old shoes...ascending to heaven" on the streets. This was the sedan chair carriers warning pedestrians to be careful of the approaching sedan chair. That's why they used a shortened sound, saying "sedan chair...ascending to heaven." Unexpectedly, now these many "old shoes" have really ascended to heaven. Because since the bridge was demolished, rickshaws have become popular on the streets. It has been a long time since we saw these many "old shoes." Isn't this really ascending to heaven?

(2) Horizontal Winnowing Cart

Songjiang people call rickshaws "yellow winnowing carts." Unexpectedly, this "yellow winnowing cart" has truly lived up to its name. Why? Because the streets of Songjiang are still made of unbreakable stone slabs, and there are many uneven places. This kind of rickshaw, pulled on uneven roads, bumps up and down. If you are not careful, you will be winnowed out to the side of the road. Isn't this "winnowing cart" living up to its name?

Snippets of Dog Catching in Suzhou 238

— Gao Cen Zhu

Suzhou has been catching stray dogs since the time when Yin Shisheng was the director of the Public Security Bureau. However, due to the opposition of local philanthropists, it never came to fruition. After Zou Xiaogong took over, he believed that stray dogs hindered sanitation and harmed people. In fact, the elimination could not be delayed. After being approved by the bureau's meeting recently, it was announced that the registration procedures for domestic dogs would be completed. The capturing started in the East District first a few days ago. There are many interesting stories. Now, I will pick up and record some of them as follows.

Dogs Do Jump Over Walls: The shelter for stray dogs in the East District is in the garden behind the ancestral hall in Aimen Lane. Reed sheds are built on both sides for the dogs to rest. The walls on all sides are not very high. Some fierce and frightened dogs can climb on the shed and jump over the wall. As the saying goes, "People will jump over beams in desperation, and dogs will jump over walls in desperation." This is true.

Dog Car Surrounded Fore and Aft: The tool for catching dogs is a three- to four-foot-long bamboo tube with a rattan ring tied to one end. Whenever a stray dog is seen, it is looped around its neck and pulled tight so that it cannot escape. Then, its feet are lifted and stuffed into the dog car. The car can hold three or four dogs. After being captured, the car is pushed all the way to the shelter. Several policemen follow, and there are also spectators surrounding and pushing forward. The stray dogs in the car are treated as if they were encountering such a thing. It is enough to be proud of.

Stray Dogs Flee in All Directions: This time, the capture of stray dogs is not being carried out simultaneously throughout the city. Therefore, the dogs in the East District are fleeing to other districts. Whenever they see policemen wearing black uniforms and white-rimmed hats, they run away in desperation. Those who catch dogs are all these policemen. Who can say that animals have no spirit?

Obstacles in Dog Catching: The capture of dogs should be carried out simultaneously throughout the city to achieve the effect of catching them all at once. The reason why they are capturing in different districts and building stray dog shelters first is all due to the advocacy of the Buddhist Association of Wu County. With this obstacle, it is impossible to do it thoroughly. Therefore, from the perspective of one corner of the East District, although they are said to be caught, stray dogs are still wandering on the market, and there are still many of them.

Customs Kill People 239

— Yan Qian

We all know that customs can influence people. But I have never heard of them killing people. I will record them in Free Talk.

The Custom of Burning Paper Money: The saying that Qingming is as important as the New Year is widely spread. But no place is as strict as Songjiang and Shanghai. Every Qingming, in addition to worshiping at the ancestral tombs, you must burn paper money at the homes of relatives. Burning paper money is commonly called "burning grass paper money." Grass paper money is made of rice straw tied into a flat and round object about a foot in diameter, filled with mountain paper money ingots, and covered with flowers cut from red and green paper. People hold this and go back and forth to each other as a great gift. It is said that stopping burning paper money is tantamount to declaring the severance of kinship. The relatives never make appointments on the same day. Therefore, there is always someone coming to each house, and every household is busy buying fish and meat. According to people's estimates, it costs at least fifteen yuan to get through this as-big-as-New Year's festival. In a world where disasters are frequent, goods are expensive, and life is difficult, how can people not complain?

Customs Kill People: In a rural village in Nanhui, south of Shanghai, a farmer's wife surnamed Mou was extremely poor because of repeated disasters. She could only fill her stomach with red flower porridge. Red flower is purple cloud clover. Farmers use it as green fertilizer. But this woman used it to fill her stomach. One day at noon, a guest arrived. The guest came holding grass paper money. According to the custom, the woman should be busy entertaining the guest. But she had nothing to offer. In a moment of panic, another guest arrived. The woman's anxiety cannot be described. In a mixture of resentment and shame, she had a thought of death. On one hand, she reluctantly entertained the guests. After inviting them to sit down, she turned and went to the back room, as if preparing something to entertain them. Who knew that she had hanged herself on the broken bed at this time? The guests waited for a long time and did not see her come out. They called her but she did not answer. They began to think it was strange. They went in together to look and saw that she had stuck out her tongue and widened her eyes, showing that she could not express her suffering and hatred. If it were not for this custom, the woman would not have thought of committing suicide even if she was poor. Is it too much to say that customs kill people?

Two Ancient Towers in the West 240

— Ji Qin

Egyptian Pyramid: The pyramids of Egypt are called "Pyramid." According to legend, they were built during the reign of King Khufu in 3124 BC. They occupy more than 20 acres of land and are about 450 feet high. The number of workers and the time required are even more shocking. It took more than 20 years from the beginning of construction to completion, and more than 300,000 craftsmen were hired. To this day, when you pass by its ancient capital, you can still see it standing tall, which is a sigh of the world's unprecedented large building.

Leaning Tower of Rome: Near the city of Sack, Italy, there is a leaning tower called Albarke. The whole body is made of granite and is 270 feet high. The top and the base were deliberately made to be inclined when they were built. From a distance, it looks like it is about to collapse. All travelers from afar will change color when they first pass through this place and dare not linger below it. In fact, the tower has been built for thousands of years and is as solid as new and has never been repaired. This is also amazing.

Warmth in My Heart (162) 241

— Bao Tian Xiao

Chapter Ten: Red Flames Soar to the Sky, a Filial Daughter Admires the Stage / Red Carpet on the Ground, Meeting Famous Actors on the Spot

It turned out that at that time, there was a group of Japanese students. Several comrades who liked to study drama gathered together and formed a drama club, which was the Qingliu Society. At first, when they were in Japan, they would occasionally perform in a small theater when there were some commemorative days. They called it the "Love Beauty Drama." It was just a few students who were interested in drama and played around casually. It was like playing tickets in Chinese old operas, and they would occasionally come to a rehearsal guest appearance or something. It also caused a commotion in the study abroad community. At this time, Chinese drama did not have the trend of male and female co-performance. Therefore, there were no women in male troupes. All the characters dressed as dan roles were male. There were several dan roles in Peking opera. After putting on makeup, they were simply like women. You couldn't tell that he was a man. And the people who supported dan roles regarded them as women, no matter what kind of lyrics, poems, or essays they wrote. It was confusing. Therefore, there was a class of people called "young masters" in the north. At that time, there was another faction of women who performed dramas, which was initially called "fashionable children's operas" and later called "Kun roles." They could not appear on stage with male actors. Therefore, the male roles in their dramas were also filled by Kun actresses. They actually wore beards and appeared on stage in robes and hats. It just felt like they had female voices and female breaths. They were a bit out of sync in terms of vision and hearing. I don't need to mention them for now. As for the newly emerging dramas, the female roles in them were also played by men. There was a Hunanese in this Qingliu Society. These two were both handsome and radiant, like willows in spring. They were all beautiful men among the Japanese students. Because they were fluttering in the world, they naturally looked beautiful and outstanding after dressing up as women. It was because they were as radiant as spring willows that the Qingliu Society lived up to its name. In addition, some people were supposed to play young men, some were supposed to play old men, and some were even born with an old woman's face. They could only play old women in dramas. They were also matched appropriately. They were also very particular about makeup. This was not like the makeup in old dramas. A traitorous minister had a white face, and Cao Cao had to draw a cross on his face. All the generals, etc., had strange faces in red, black, green, and blue. The makeup in new dramas was just embellished according to the shapes of modern people, or imitated according to the identity of the people in the drama. However, beauties, celebrities, villains, and heroes also had to be evident in their faces. At this time, several members of the Qingliu Society had returned to the country. They were preparing to give a public performance in Shanghai. Because several classmates had returned to China, those who were farmers and friends in the interior had to go back to visit their families. Some had already found some jobs and would soon go to work. While everyone was not dispersed, it was necessary to give a public performance.

River Rice Market Declines 250

Zhabei: Yesterday, the source of goods from the inland routes continued to be strong. It is estimated that the number of cargo ships arriving in the port within two days will be around fifty. Buyers have largely turned to a wait-and-see attitude, and the sales market is extremely quiet. High-grade Northern Jiangsu rice uniformly fell by 0.15 to 0.2 yuan, and sellers were also eager to sell. The situation for rice has now changed, and it would not be surprising if subsequent prices were to decline. Thin rice varieties are not in demand, with prices slightly below 0.02 yuan, and the market conditions are extremely quiet. Due to limited arrivals of Yangxian rice, sales were sluggish, but prices remained relatively stable due to solid ground. Dujian Zhunjiān rice was stagnant and quiet, with prices falling by about 0.01 yuan. Only high-quality goods for distribution were active, while the trend for mid-range goods was very weak. The arrival and sales of Bianyuan rice were both sluggish. Although the prices of Geng and Xian rice varieties had risen, Baiyuan rice had not been able to follow the trend and prosper. Therefore, even with the decline in prices, Yuánmǐ rice remained stable.

South Shanghai: River cargo arrivals were observed, approximately twenty ships. Sales in this area are largely stagnant. Changshu Baigeng rice fell by 0.15 yuan, while Suzhou Tongji rice fell by varying amounts, from 0.02 to 0.03 yuan, with strong selling pressure. The market is gradually reversing. The thin early rice from Southern Jiangsu, which had experienced a false increase at the end of last month, is now being affected by increased arrivals and a soft market in Zhabei. Sales are increasingly weak, with large quantities being sold at discounts of over 0.02 yuan. Transaction volumes for the entire day were scarce, indicating sluggish buying appetite. The amount of Yangxian rice in storage and arrival remains limited, and sales are still active. While Du Zi Xian rice and various other Xian rice varieties from other regions are inquired about, transactions are only small and sporadic. Since foreign rice prices are still low, sellers are unwilling to repair the previous prices. However, reports indicate that the next batch of foreign rice will arrive, and the buying appetite from both local and foreign buyers has weakened. Consequently, the price of local Xian rice has declined, dropping by 0.01 yuan. The market for Yinhua Tongbian rice remains consistent, with buyers only selecting ordinary

varieties for slight purchases, and prices barely maintaining their original levels.

Group News 261

Church Holds Hymn Concert

The Russian Christian Hymn Society announces that the Society will hold a hymn concert at the Nanjing Road Municipal Hall today (April 3rd) at 9:15 PM. The program is divided into three sections. The first and third sections are choral performances by the Society's choir, solo recitals of Russian famous poems and songs, and trio performances. The second section will feature choruses of Mozart and Gounod's Requiem and Ave Maria by the choir, and Fan Hualin's harmony on the piano. The most brilliant part of the program is the Russian Martyrs, composed by Maestro Masbim. Tikbon composed the song for the people seeking assistance during the Russian famine. Tikbon was the first person to protect the church and oppose the Communist Party, and later died in prison for openly resisting the Communist Party. Tonight, Mr. Blcchin will sing the words of Mr. Tikbon seeking help from the world for the people, which was composed into a song by Mr. Masbin, etc.

Dog Show Scheduled

The China Kennel Club announces that this year's dog show is scheduled for Saturday, May 17, still at the Shanghai Racecourse. Membership forms for entering dogs in the competition have been printed and can be obtained from Mr. Ge Lin of Eagle Steelworks, 8 Museum Road. Please fill them out and submit them as soon as possible in order to be classified. This year's dog show is intended to increase the interest in buying dogs and to reward various excellent dogs produced in China. Various competition methods have been specially added. However, concerted efforts are needed to rectify and improve, so that this exhibition can be promoted vigorously and become a grand event, etc.

Theater News 263

Glorious Theater Premieres "Glamorous Prince" Today

The Glorious Theater at 21 Museum Road announces that the theater is Shanghai's leading sound film theater, with beautiful decorations, comfortable seats, excellent sound, and harmonious temperature control. Starting today, the theater will premiere Paramount's colorful sound and dance masterpiece, "Glamorous Prince." The female lead, Mary Eaton, is the female lead in the previous hit film "A Clever Matchmaker," which sold out for two weeks. Her singing and dancing skills are praised as all-round talents on Broadway. This film is also Eaton's carefully structured representative work, full of concentration, focus, and inspiration. The plot is glamorous and romantic, the background is gorgeous and luxurious, and there are also the songs of Helen Morgan, the star of "Show Boat," the songs of radio music star Rudy Vallée, and the humor of comedian Eddie Cantor, which makes people laugh. Such a good film is truly worth watching a hundred times. The film has been inspected and approved by the Shanghai Special Municipality Film Inspection Committee, etc.

Meiyun Troupe to Perform "Seven Emotions" Tomorrow

The Meihua Dance Troupe announces that the fourth performance of the troupe will be held at the Nanjing Road Municipal Hall for two days starting tomorrow, performing the glamorous and grand dance drama "Seven Emotions." More than 30 male and female actors will sing and dance together

at the same time, which is unusually lively. The plot is tense and bizarre. The play was written by the troupe leader, Ms. Wei Rongbo, and composed by Mr. Cai Wenjin. The lyrics are new and the tune is melodious, conveying joy, anger, sorrow, happiness, love, hate, and desire in clear songs and graceful dances. The play has been rehearsed for three months, and the costumes and scenery cost more than 3,000 yuan, etc.

Lehua Company Goes to Suzhou and Hangzhou to Shoot On Location

The main male roles in "The Shadow of the Empty Valley," produced by Lehua Film Company, are played by big stars such as Huang Zhen, Chen Yulou, Lu Lele, and Lu Yun. The company departed today for Suzhou and Hangzhou to shoot on location, etc.

Medical News 264

Li Boqi Comes to Shanghai to Open a Clinic

Li Boqi, a famous doctor from Dong'ou, has profound medical knowledge and is particularly skilled in typhoid fever, gynecology, and pediatrics. This time, he is traveling through Shanghai and has only agreed to stay for a month. He is now practicing medicine at No. 9, Lane 3, Gui'anli, Bei Chujia Bridge, French Concession.

Hualong Chinese Medicine Hospital Opens

The Shanghai South Society announces that the famous doctor Ding Jiwan has a high reputation in Shanghai and has been practicing medicine for many years. In order to promote Chinese medicine and benefit the poor and sick, he has specially established Hualong Chinese Medicine Hospital at No. 48, Huage Road, at the intersection of Edward Road, French Concession. The hospital is fully equipped and large in scale. Invitation cards were issued yesterday, and the opening ceremony is scheduled for 2:00 PM on April 1st.

Expansion of Ningxin Hospital

Ningxin Obstetrics Hospital declares that Ms. Zhang Qingfu is an obstetrician who has always been skilled in obstetrics. She founded this hospital in Deyuli, Nanjing Road, more than ten years ago, and has a good reputation. Recently, because the original site had too few delivery rooms, those who came later often regretted not being able to find a place. The hospital has specially moved to the new house at No. 45 in the back of the alley, and more than ten large and small delivery rooms have been added upstairs. The rooms face the flower garden, the air is fresh and clean, and the sunlight is sufficient. The equipment is designed with the needs of pregnant women in mind, comprehensive and comfortable. Whether it is difficult labor or normal labor, Ms. Zhang performs the surgery herself with sincerity and stability, and the fees are very low, which is especially beneficial to the common people. Those who want to give birth to a Ningxin child, please pay attention, etc.

Publishing News 265

"Cres" Newspaper Published Today

"Cres" tri-weekly newspaper, co-edited by Mr. Hu Xiongfei and Mr. Chen Tingchao, focuses on glamorous arts and literature, establishing a unique style that is extraordinary. The contributors are all well-known writers. The inaugural issue is published today, and the text and photos are extremely exciting. Free copies of three issues are available for out-of-town readers. Please send two cents for postage to the address next to the Far East Hotel, 6th Avenue, etc.

"Min Ming Monthly" Finance Issue Published

"Min Ming Monthly" announces that the finance issue of the magazine contains articles such as Zi Yaohua's "Relieving the Silver Price and Unifying the Silver Standard," Liu Xizhe's "Reforming the Currency System and Commercial Rights," Chen Zhenyi's "From the Defects of the Gold Standard System and Monetary Studies, Researching China's Currency System," Xiang Mo'an's "The Advantages and Disadvantages of the New Gold Unit of Customs," Wang Yiwen's "The Fundamental Theory of Relieving the Financial Panic of Silver Price Decline," Li Boqin's "Investigation of the Alloy of Currencies in Various Countries," Sun Naizhan's "The Changes in the Currency Standard in the Stage of Economic Evolution," and Li Chou Peng's "The Issue of Saving Movement and Gold Price Increase," totaling fifteen or sixteen articles, all with unique insights, detailed plans, and rich content, etc.
